\"is_shared\": true}]}], \"dashboard_html\": \"\"};\n        \n        const categoryIcons = {\n            'Utilities': '',\n            'Transit & Roads': '',\n            'Emergency Alerts': '',\n            'Local News': '',\n            'Economic Indicators': '',\n            'Aviation': ''\n        };\n        \n        function renderMunicipalities(filteredData) {\n            const grid = document.getElementById('municipalityGrid');\n            const noResults = document.getElementById('noResults');\n            \n            if (filteredData.length === 0) {\n                grid.style.display = 'none';\n                noResults.style.display = 'block';\n                return;\n            }\n            \n            grid.style.display = 'grid';\n            noResults.style.display = 'none';\n            \n            grid.innerHTML = filteredData.map(muni => {\n                const isShared = muni.name === 'Shared/Regional';\n                const sharedClass = isShared ? 'shared' : '';\n                \n                // Group sources by category\n                const categorized = {};\n                muni.data_sources.forEach(source => {\n                    const cat = source.category || 'Other';\n                    if (!categorized[cat]) categorized[cat] = [];\n                    categorized[cat].push(source);\n                });\n                \n                const categories = Object.keys(categorized).sort();\n                \n                return `\n                    <div class=\"municipality-card ${sharedClass}\" data-municipality=\"${muni.name}\">\n                        <h2 class=\"municipality-name\">\n                            ${isShared ? '' : ''} ${muni.name}\n                            <span class=\"badge\">${muni.data_sources.length} sources</span>\n                        </h2>\n                        \n                        ${categories.map(category => `\n                            <div class=\"category-section\" data-category=\"${category}\">\n                                <h3 class=\"category-title\">\n                                    ${categoryIcons[category] || ''} ${category}\n                                    <span class=\"badge\">${categorized[category].length}</span>\n                                </h3>\n                                <div class=\"sources-grid\">\n                                    ${categorized[category].map(source => `\n                                        <a href=\"${source.url}\" \n                                           target=\"_blank\" \n                                           class=\"source-card ${source.is_shared ? 'shared-badge' : ''}\"\n                                           data-source-name=\"${source.source_name}\"\n                                           data-description=\"${source.description || ''}\">\n                                            <div class=\"source-name\">${source.source_name}</div>\n                                            ${source.description ? `<div class=\"source-description\">${source.description}</div>` : ''}\n                                            <div class=\"source-url\">${source.url}</div>\n                                        </a>\n                                    `).join('')}\n                                </div>\n                            </div>\n                        `).join('')}\n                    </div>\n                `;\n            }).join('');\n        }\n        \n        function filterData() {\n            const searchTerm = document.getElementById('searchInput').value.toLowerCase();\n            const muniFilter = document.getElementById('municipalityFilter').value;\n            const catFilter = document.getElementById('categoryFilter').value;\n            \n            let filtered = DATA.municipalities;\n            \n            // Filter by municipality\n            if (muniFilter) {\n                filtered = filtered.filter(m => m.name === muniFilter);\n            }\n            \n            // Filter by search term or category\n            if (searchTerm || catFilter) {\n                filtered = filtered.map(muni => {\n                    let sources = muni.data_sources;\n                    \n                    if (catFilter) {\n                        sources = sources.filter(s => s.category === catFilter);\n                    }\n                    \n                    if (searchTerm) {\n                        sources = sources.filter(s => \n                            s.source_name.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm) ||\n                            (s.description && s.description.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm)) ||\n                            s.url.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm)\n                        );\n                    }\n                    \n                    return { ...muni, data_sources: sources };\n                }).filter(m => m.data_sources.length > 0);\n            }\n            \n            renderMunicipalities(filtered);\n        }\n        \n        // Initialize\n        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {\n            // Populate municipality filter\n            const muniFilter = document.getElementById('municipalityFilter');\n            DATA.municipalities.forEach(muni => {\n                const option = document.createElement('option');\n                option.value = muni.name;\n                option.textContent = muni.name;\n                muniFilter.appendChild(option);\n            });\n            \n            // Calculate total sources\n            const totalSources = DATA.municipalities.reduce((sum, m) => {\n                const localSources = m.data_sources.filter(s => !s.is_shared);\n                return sum + localSources.length;\n            }, 0);\n            document.getElementById('totalSources').textContent = totalSources;\n            \n            // Event listeners\n            document.getElementById('searchInput').addEventListener('input', filterData);\n            document.getElementById('municipalityFilter').addEventListener('change', filterData);\n            document.getElementById('categoryFilter').addEventListener('change', filterData);\n            \n            // Initial render\n            renderMunicipalities(DATA.municipalities);\n        });\n    </script>\n</body>\n</html>"
